msg:TLDR: Had really high expectations when I booked this 5 diamond hotel, however the stay experience fell short from the expectations.

The Good:
+ Was offered room upgrade to sea view room during checked in.
+ Interior and exterior design of the hotel is really sets a relaxing tone to the entire stay. 
+ It was a nice touch having Bellboys to help us with luggage and open doors whenever we arrive at the hotel lobby
+ Staffs and cleaners greeted us was also a nice touch 
+ Breakfast options are extensive (including fresh juice bar and daily special juice concoction)
+ Free hotel activities to do daily 
+ Gym is well maintained and a good number of machines 

The Bad
- (Presales) Didn‚Äôt appreciate the fact that the booking page didn‚Äôt state the hotel deposit amount (which is slightly more than 1 time the hotel room price) and was only mentioned during check-in. Prior the trip, I tried to ask about whether there‚Äôs any hotel deposit via Trip.com message to hotel function and there‚Äôs no reply at all. (I mean a 3 diamond star hotel I stayed previous replied‚Ä¶ but a 5 diamond star hotel didn‚Äôt).
- (Not controllable) Sadly, there‚Äôs construction going on and can see cranes and construction machinery hindering the view of the sea, as well as the noises.
- There‚Äôs supposedly a butler assigned to each guest, but my butler only added me on WeChat several hours after checkin. Also, was asking the butler about one of the afternoon hotel was still going on as we reached the venue and there‚Äôs no one around. He said he will check and then no reply for 20mins before I messaged him to inform that we won‚Äôt be waiting anymore. Didn‚Äôt appreciate that there‚Äôs no follow up. 
- The shower control knob will suddenly fall off at certain angle which can be rather dangerous given that it has quite a weight to it. 
- The bathtub‚Äôs shower head keeps leaking when we turned the other tap on to fill the bathtub, and we had to put the shower head into the bathtub to prevent flooding. 

All in all, it fell short on expectations in terms of the service compared to the service my partner and I had experienced in a 3 diamond star hotel at a fraction of this hotel‚Äôs price. 

Nonetheless, it is really a gorgeous place to stay in. Tastefully decorated and smell really great. Most of the staffs are friendly.

msg:A hotel focusing on environmental protection concepts
At first I thought it would be like many hotels with a concept.
But every day I stayed there, I quietly discovered that this hotel is really doing environmental protection attentively.
First of all, in terms of hotel decoration details, it ranges from the selection of building materials, the use of a lot of recycled wood and volcanic stone, to the use of natural plants to decorate the exterior walls, and even the slippers and clothes hangers in the room are recyclable materials.
Moreover, the hotel also has its own system for saving water and energy. When I visited the hotel, I also found that there were many abandoned large tree trunks on some grasslands, which were like art installations and seemed to tell their own annual ring stories.
I remember seeing a very profound sentence in the promotional video in the elevator: "We do not ask for, but respectfully pick up nature's gifts."
So you saw the design of the birch branches crossing the roof in the lobby
I saw various decorative walls made of discarded wooden *****s in the elevator hall.

In addition, the most popular thing about the hotel is probably the fully transparent infinity swimming pool.
The afternoon sun shines through the water onto the ground floor, creating sparkling light and shadow.

In addition, the breakfast in the hotel is also excellent.
Sanya specialty noodles that are different every day are really fun to eat
And the fruits and vegetables are all delivered from our own farm.
If you are a bread person, you will also love their various handmade breads and my favorite Banlan sauce.
In the end, what made me completely fall in love with this hotel was the service.
I have always felt that both design and style are good
Everyone has different preferences

It really warmed me up

Makes me feel at home in the hotel

Although the hotel is not so famous or famous among the many luxury hotels in Haitang Bay,

Sunshine 1 is relatively new, but it's not like the Maotai Hotel next door, which just opened this year. After learning that I had not left the hotel the next day, they brought a large plate of fruit and 1 hotel logo chocolate!

In fact, since 2020, I have wanted to experience #SanyaSunshineOneHotel[topic]#, because the concept of environmental protection is the main concept here, which coincides with the concept of divers who love nature and the sea.
ü™µThe decoration items of the hotel are basically made of wood and rattan. In order to reduce the generation of plastic products, the door card is made into a round cute wooden sign with a chip.
ü™®The design materials for the exterior wall of the hotel include abandoned ship wood and rail sleepers from the seaside of Sanya, volcanic rocks from Haikou, and blue bricks and black tiles of old houses transported from Hubei. In order to reduce ecological pollution, decorations made from recycled waste such as iron sheets and tree stumps can be seen everywhere when walking in the hotel.
üçÉThe water supply system in the lobby wall continues to support the growth of green plants on the wall, making people feel like they are in a tropical rain forest.
‚ôªÔ∏èThe cups used in the room are all made of recycled old wine bottles after secondary cutting, the toothbrush handle in the bathroom is pure wood, and other disposable items are also intimately reminding the guests to use their imagination to give these disposables Supplies have a second life, thereby reducing the use of single-use items.
This is the first Sunshine One Hotel in China by the founder of W Hotel, and there are only five in the world. It may not be regarded as a traditional five-star resort hotel for many people, but it is completely in line with my view of vacation. All kinds of needs, many small details full of design sense and extraordinary significance continue to surprise us. Sitting at the sky bar on the 9th floor at night blowing the sea breeze seems to be in Bangkok's midnight lounge, standing on the balcony during the day or in the floating swimming pool. Looking at the blue sea, tension and anxiety can be released one by one.
üí∞ In November, all major hotels in Sanya are on special prices. The usual basic room rate is now directly in the boutique sea view room. The recent price is in the early 1000s, including double breakfast.

Although I have not been able to come due to various reasons before, this time I think it is the best arrangement. Our family spent two days that were unforgettable and pleasant. For me, leisure can be regarded as a good holiday experience, and quietness must be a necessary prerequisite. During the off-season, the number of people in the public areas of the hotel is basically less than ten. Due to the small number of guests, the service quality has also been greatly improved, allowing our whole family to get a very attentive service experience. The three outdoor swimming pools of different depths meet the needs of everyone in our family. The breakfast is also rich and exquisite, which is very popular in my heart. My favorite is the bathrobes in the room with novel design but super practical and easy to wear. Go downstairs to the lobby You can even buy the same model to take home. When we left, the staff also gave us a straw hat in the store as a souvenir, which was really thoughtful.
‚ù§Ô∏èOverall we are very satisfied and looking forward to our next stay! If you also want to come to Sanya, come here and give yourself a vacation!
